<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;2.02. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Disclosure of Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On January&#160;30, 2020 we issued the press release attached as Exhibit 99.1. It is incorporated into this report by reference. The press release describes the results of our operations for the quarter ended December&#160;31, 2019. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;8.01. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Other Events.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;margin-right:2%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On January&#160;30, 2020 we announced that our board of directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of US $0.39 per share. The dividend will have a record date of February&#160;13, 2020, payable on March&#160;19, 2020. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#8217;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of Chess Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <span style="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</span> date will be February&#160;12, 2020, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#8217;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from February&#160;12, 2020, through February&#160;13, 2020, inclusive.&#160;</p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Item&#160;9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Exhibits </p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-size:10pt;border-collapse:separate;border-spacing:0;width:100%;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto">

<td></td>
<td></td>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ResMed Inc. Announces Results for the Second Quarter of Fiscal Year 2020 </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Year-over-year revenue grows 13%, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating profit up 21%</I>
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Balanced growth across product portfolio, software solutions, and global markets</I> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Note: A webcast of ResMed&#146;s conference call will be available at 4:30 p.m. ET today at <U>http://investor.resmed.com</U> </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SAN DIEGO, January&nbsp;30, 2020 &#150; ResMed Inc. (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD), a world-leading digital health company, today announced results for its quarter
ended December&nbsp;31, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Second Quarter 2020 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased 13% to $736.2&nbsp;million; up 14% on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP gross margin of 58.0%; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margin expanded 60 bps to
59.7% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net operating profit increased 26%; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating profit up 21%
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP diluted earnings per share of $1.10; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per
share of $1.21 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We had a strong December quarter with double-digit <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> growth and
further gross margin expansion, as well as continued fiscal discipline that resulted in improvements in operating leverage and double-digit growth at the bottom line,&#148; said Mick Farrell, ResMed&#146;s CEO. &#147;We are seeing continued strong
customer demand for our new products, particularly in masks and accessories with another quarter of high-teens growth in that category. ResMed is continuing to lead in digital health as we transform lives in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> healthcare, leading the innovation of medical devices and software that improve health outcomes, create efficiencies, and reduce overall healthcare system costs. With over 100&nbsp;million
lives improved in 2019, and strong growth ahead, we&#146;re well on our way to improving 250&nbsp;million lives in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> healthcare in 2025.&#148; </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In order to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of
foreign currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency basis,&#148; which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we
translate the current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to
U.S. dollar measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Other Business and Operational Highlights </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

Home Health and Hospice platform as its preferred solution to integrate with its Cerner Millenium<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> electronic health record. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Introduced AirFit N30, the world&#146;s first tube-down nasal cradle CPAP mask with a front-facing tube, a brand
new option for sleep apnea treatment. Other key features include an adjustable elastic headgear, a nasal cradle cushion that sits under the nasal bridge to eliminate soreness, and a curved design to provide a secure seal regardless of how the wearer
sleeps or moves. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Announced an upgraded AirView for Respiratory program that provides HMEs and physicians with quicker access to
essential respiratory patient data, including more granular clinical data and respiration trends, and management by exception, allowing them to provide better care. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Agreed in January to acquire SnapWorx, a privately held software company providing patient contact management and
workflow optimization for the sleep apnea resupply market. SnapWorx&#146;s software platform automates workflow and document retrieval in ways that complement Brightree&#146;s industry-leading, multi-channel resupply solution. The combination of
Brightree ReSupply&#146;s technology and live call services with SnapWorx creates the most comprehensive set of resupply solutions in the industry. The transaction is expected to close shortly. It is expected to be initially neutral to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings per share, and accretive to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings per share in fiscal year 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Dividend program </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The ResMed board of directors
today declared a quarterly cash dividend of $0.39 per share. The dividend will have a record date of February&nbsp;13, 2020, payable on March&nbsp;19, 2020. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock trading
on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of Chess Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1
ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</FONT> date will be February&nbsp;12, 2020, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#146;s settlement operating
rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from February&nbsp;12, 2020, through February&nbsp;13, 2020, inclusive.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P>

telephone replay will be available until February&nbsp;13, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>About ResMed </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier,
higher-quality lives. Our cloud-connected medical devices transform care for people with sleep apnea, COPD, and other chronic diseases. Our comprehensive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT>
software platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting of their choice. By enabling better care, we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease, and lower costs for
consumers and healthcare systems in more than 140 countries.&nbsp;To learn more, visit <U>ResMed.com</U> and follow @ResMed. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Safe harbor statement

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">ResMed adjusts for the impact of the amortization of acquired intangibles, deferred revenue fair value
adjustment, litigation settlement expenses, acquisition-related expenses, and the impact of U.S. tax reform on income tax expense from their evaluation of ongoing operations, and believes that investors benefit from adjusting these items to
facilitate a more meaningful evaluation of current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ResMed believes that <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share is an additional measure of performance that investors can use to compare operating results between reporting periods. ResMed uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
information internally in planning, forecasting, and evaluating the results of operations in the current period and in comparing it to past periods. ResMed believes this information provides investors better insight when evaluating ResMed&#146;s
performance from core operations and provides consistent financial reporting. The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures is intended to supplement, and not to replace, the presentation of net income and other GAAP measures.
Like all <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings are subject to inherent limitations because they do not include all the expenses that must be included under GAAP. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In order to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of
foreign currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency basis,&#148; which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we
translate the current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to
U.S. dollar measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
